 * _Added_
    *  **+** [amphicoelous](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_3000717) *[comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment)* The tuatara spine is made up of hourglass-shaped amphicoelous vertebrae, concave both before and behind. This is the usual condition of fish vertebrae and some amphibians, but is unique to tuatara within the amniotes[Wikipedia].

    *  **-** [capsule of lymph node](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0002194) **SubClassOf** [has part](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000051) **some** [connective tissue](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0002384)
    *  **-** [capsule of lymph node](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0002194) **SubClassOf** [surrounds](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/RO_0002221) **some** [lymph node](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0000029)
 * _Added_

### New ObjectProperty : [bounding layer of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/RO_0002007)

 * [bounding layer of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/RO_0002007) *[label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label)* bounding layer of
 * [bounding layer of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/RO_0002007) *[comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment)* A relationship that applies between a continuant and its outer, bounding layer.  Examples include the relationship between a multicellular organism and its integument, between an animal cell and its plasma membrane, and between a membrane bound organelle and its outer/bounding membrane.
 * [bounding layer of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/RO_0002007) *[database cross reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref)* RO:0002007
 * [bounding layer of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/RO_0002007) *[id](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#id)* bounding_layer_of
 * [bounding layer of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/RO_0002007) *[shorthand](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#shorthand)* bounding_layer_of
 * [bounding layer of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/RO_0002007) *[has obo namespace](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasOBONamespace)* uberon
 * SubObjectPropertyOf( [bounding layer of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/RO_0002007) [part of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000050) ) 
 * [bounding layer of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/RO_0002007) *[definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115)* X outer_layer_of Y iff:
. X :continuant that bearer_of some PATO:laminar
. X part_of Y
. exists Z :surface
. X has_boundary Z
. Z boundary_of Y

has_boundary: http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/RO_0002002

### Changes for: [site_of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/core#site_of)

 * _Deleted_
    *  **-** [site of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/core#site_of) *[definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115)* C site_of P iff exists species S such that P occurs_in C for all members of S. Example: bursa of Fabricius site_of B-cell differentiation. { [database cross reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref)=GOC:cjm } 
 * _Added_
    *  **+** [site of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/core#site_of) *[definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115)* c site_of p if c is the bearer of a disposition that is realized by a process that has p as part
    *  **+** [site of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/core#site_of) *[has related synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasRelatedSynonym)* capable_of_has_part
